for la in $(find /home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot/usr/lib* -name "*.la"); do \
	cp -a "${la}" "${la}.fixed" && \
	/usr/bin/sed -i -e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:@BASE_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:@STAGING_DIR@:g" \
		 -e "s:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/usr:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/usr:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/lib:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/lib:g" \
		 -e "s:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:g" \
		-e "s:@STAGING_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:g" \
		-e "s:@BASE_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:g" \
		"${la}.fixed" && \
	if cmp -s "${la}" "${la}.fixed"; then \
		rm -f "${la}.fixed"; \
	else \
		mv "${la}.fixed" "${la}"; \
	fi || exit 1; \
done

If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
specify the full pathname of the library, or use the '-LLIBDIR'
flag during linking and do at least one of the following:

   - add LIBDIR to the 'LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable

	/usr/bin/sed -i -e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:@BASE_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:@STAGING_DIR@:g" \
		 -e "s:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/usr:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/usr:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/lib:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/lib:g" \
		 -e "s:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:g" \
		-e "s:@STAGING_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:g" \
		-e "s:@BASE_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:g" \
		"${la}.fixed" && \
	if cmp -s "${la}" "${la}.fixed"; then \
		rm -f "${la}.fixed"; \
	else \
		mv "${la}.fixed" "${la}"; \
	fi || exit 1; \
done

>>> libmicrohttpd 0.9.77 Fixing libtool files
for la in $(find /home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot/usr/lib* -name "*.la"); do \
	cp -a "${la}" "${la}.fixed" && \
	/usr/bin/sed -i -e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:@BASE_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:@STAGING_DIR@:g" \
		 -e "s:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/usr:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/usr:g" \
		-e "s:\(['= ]\)/lib:\\1@STAGING_DIR@/lib:g" \
		 -e "s:@TOOLCHAIN_EXTERNAL_INSTALL_DIR@:/opt/toolchain/Xuantie-900-gcc-linux-6.6.0-glibc-x86_64-V2.10.1:g" \
		-e "s:@STAGING_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig/host/riscv64-buildroot-linux-gnu/sysroot:g" \
		-e "s:@BASE_DIR@:/home/phebe/k230d/k230_linux_sdk/output/k230d_canmv_defconfig:g" \
		"${la}.fixed" && \
	if cmp -s "${la}" "${la}.fixed"; then \
		rm -f "${la}.fixed"; \
	else \
		mv "${la}.fixed" "${la}"; \
	fi || exit 1; \
done
